***lat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lat.html>lat</a> (14822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>latte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*latta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lattō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laþþō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lat.html>lat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:latten.html>latten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:latje.html>latje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A slate, a lath.</li>
<li>A specifically, the common shortening of <a href = vnd.unilang:meetlat.html>meetlat</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> ruler, yardstick.</li></ol>

***laten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> (108)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lātan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*lātan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lētaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave, to cause to remain in the same position or state
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lieten.html>lieten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b>left</b> it like that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave, to allow to remain/continue to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>Laat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Just <b>leave</b> it lying there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to let, to allow to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lieten.html>lieten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b>let</b> him go.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to, to make; <span class="use-with-mention">Creates a causative phrase.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:liet.html>liet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spullen.html>spullen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He dropped his stuff on the ground.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to may, to let; <span class="use-with-mention">forms a optative phrase.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>Laat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Let</b> there be light.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***latrine.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrine</a> (24484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrine</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrine</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lātrīna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bath; <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrine</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:latrines.html>latrines</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrinetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a very simple <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a> facility, usually just a pit or trench; a <a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrine</a>.</li></ol>

***latte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>latte</a> (29229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>latte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>latte</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">late</i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> source, probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*latta</i>; see also German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>Latte</a></i>, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lat.html>lat</a></i>, and English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lath</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lattice</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>latte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr">lattes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lath</li>
<li>slat</li>
<li>ruler (measuring device)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shoe; foot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hit, puff</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ski</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:batten.html>batten</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>latte</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:enkelvoud.html>enkelvoud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verleden.html>verleden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>  <a href = vnd.unilang:latten.html>latten</a><br />
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>latte</a></b>.</i> <br /></li>

***laudanum.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laudanum.html>laudanum</a> (28664)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paracelsus" class="extiw" title="w:Paracelsus">Paracelsus</a> for a tincture he made containing opium, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">laudō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I praise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ladanum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a gum resin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λάδανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ládanon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally the same word as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ladanum</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">labdanum</i>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:laudanum.html>laudanum</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">laudano</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">ladano</i>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ladanum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:laudanum.html>laudanum</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">laudanums</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A tincture of opium, once widely used for various medical purposes and as a recreational drug.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutchman.html>Dutchman</a>'s <a href = vnd.unilang:laudanum.html>laudanum</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:laudanum.html>laudanum</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">laudanums</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">laudanuming</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">laudanumed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To add <a href = vnd.unilang:laudanum.html>laudanum</a> to (a <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> or the like).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cause (a person) to be high on <a href = vnd.unilang:laudanum.html>laudanum</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:laudanum.html>laudanum</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li>opiumtinctuur, <a href = vnd.unilang:vroeger.html>vroeger</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruikt.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geneesmiddel.html>geneesmiddel</a></li></ol>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
</body>

***lauw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lauw.html>lauw</a> (26606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lâeu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lāo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlēwaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>lukewarm (<a href = vnd.unilang:temperaturen.html>temperature</a>)</li>

***lavement.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lavement.html>lavement</a> (51426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lavament</i>. Borrowed from Old French or Latin. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lavare</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lavement.html>lavement</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lavement.html>lavementen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lavement.html>lavementje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:lawine.html>Lawine</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alemannic_German" class="extiw" title="w:Alemannic German">Alemannic German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gsw">Lauwin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">lowin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">lowin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">labina</i>, derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lābī</i>.

***lebberen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lebberen.html>lebberen</a> (60284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lepperen</i>, frequentative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">leppen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lebberen.html>lebberen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lick audibly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lap; to <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> audibly, often using a tongue

***led.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> (74741)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">liðr</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>,<sup id="cite_ref-ND_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-ND-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liþuz</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nn">ledd</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, although formerly considered alternative forms. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">liður</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a></i> and dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lith</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>definite singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:leden.html>leden</a></b>, <i>indefinite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">ledar</b>, <i>definite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">ledene</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">ledane</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a joint or a movable body part adjacent to it</li>
<li>a single part within a whole, especially a sequence
<ol><li>a link (in a chain)</li>
<li>a generation</li></ol></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_4">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hlið</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>,<sup id="cite_ref-ND_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-ND-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlidą</i>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a></i>. Ultimately rooted in the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱley-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shelter, cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>definite singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">ledet</b>, <i>indefinite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a></strong></b>, <i>definite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:leda.html>leda</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a gate</li>
<li>an opening in a fence</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4_3">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***leder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a> (9176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lether</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leþrą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*létrom</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Ledder</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">leare</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>Leder</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">leather</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">læder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>ledertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">leather</span></li>

***ledig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ledig.html>ledig</a> (49095)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lithag</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liþugaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ledig.html>ledig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ledig.html>lediger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ledigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>a formal form of <a href = vnd.unilang:leeg.html>leeg</a></i>) without content, containing nothing, empty
<ul><li>Jesse Frederik, "<a href = vnd.unilang:dode.html>Dode</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liberalen.html>liberalen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dikke.html>dikke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a>', <a href = vnd.unilang:hebzucht.html>hebzucht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> graaiers", <i>Follow the Money</i>, 2 June 2015.
<dl><dd>‘<a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>Ieder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nadenkt.html>nadenkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhoudingen.html>verhoudingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:mensch.html>mensch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:getroffen.html>getroffen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:feit.html>feit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:arbeidt.html>arbeidt</a>, arm <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:terwijl.html>terwijl</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ledig.html>ledig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:baadt.html>baadt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:overvloed.html>overvloed</a>,’ <a href = vnd.unilang:stelde.html>stelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:linden.html>Linden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a>.
<dl><dd>"Everyone who thinks about the relations between humanity and material goods, will be struck by the fact that often he who works <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> poor, while he who leads an empty life wallows in abundance," <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:linden.html>Linden</a> observed.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ledikant.html>ledikant</a> (81896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> camp</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ledikant.html>ledikant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ledikant.html>ledikanten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ledikant.html>ledikantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cot, crib <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> for children</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebied.html>gebied</a></i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lāicus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">layman, laic</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λαϊκός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">laïkós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of the people</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λαός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">laós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the people</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leen.html>leen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lēn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laihną</i>.

<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lether</i>, from<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leþrą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>leather

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lêre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lēra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laizō</i>.
</p>
